    function submitToNewsletter(el) {
      var formElement = $dnj('#newsletter_signup_form')
      if (formIsBlocked(formElement)) {
        console.log("submit to newsletter not fired. already submitted");
        return false;
      };
      console.log("submit to newsletter fired");
      $dnj.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/home/email_signup",
        data: formElement.serialize()
      }).done(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR ) {
        log("done:" + textStatus);
        log(data);
        window.scrollTo(0,0);
        if(data.errors) {
          dnDisplayMessage('error', null, data.errors)
        } else if(data.message) {
          dnDisplayMessage('success', null, data.message)
        };
        markFormUnblocked($dnj('#newsletter_signup_form'));
      }).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown ) {
        log("fail:" + textStatus);
        log(errorThrown);
        log(jqXHR);
        window.scrollTo(0,0);
        dnDisplayMessage('error', null, "Failed to add email to Newsletter list");
        markFormUnblocked($dnj('#newsletter_signup_form'));
      });
    };

        return false;

        url: "/home/email_signup",

const trigger = document.querySelector("#help-center-pop");
const modal = document.querySelector("#custompopup");
const close = document.querySelector("span.close-popup");
var body = document.body;
trigger.addEventListener("click", () => {
  modal.style.display = "block";
    body.classList.add("body-popup");
    
});
close.addEventListener("click", () => {
  modal.style.display = "none";
    body.classList.remove("body-popup");
});
jQuery('body').click(function(){
        modal.style.display = "none";
body.classList.remove("body-popup");
        });

});

jQuery(this).click(function(){
jQuery(this).toggleClass('Active');
});   
});

var  gat =  jQuery(this).html();
    jQuery(this).parents("h4.dn-styled.dn-sized.dn-below").after('<span class="dn-brand">'+gat+'</span>')
    
})

    }else{
    jQuery(".dn-filter-list").removeClass("active-filter");
    jQuery(this).parent(".dn-filter-list").addClass("active-filter");
    }
    
}) 
jQuery(".dn-product-view-container").prepend('<div class=cstm-pop-up><i class="fa-solid fa-magnifying-glass"></i></div>');
      }, 3000);
}

});

/*gsap-animation-start*/    
 gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger)
        gsap.set(".img1", {opacity:1})
        gsap.set(".img2", {opacity:0})
        gsap.set(".img3", {opacity:0})
       
        gsap.timeline({
        scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: ".main-box",
            start: "top top",
            end: "bottom bottom",
            scrub: true,
            pin:".right-box",
           
        }
        })
        gsap.to(".img2",{
            opacity: 1,
        scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: ".section2",
            start: "top bottom",
            end: "bottom bottom",
            scrub: true,
           
        }
        })
        gsap.to(".img3",{
            opacity: 1,
        scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: ".section3",
            start: "top bottom",
            end: "bottom bottom",
            scrub: true,
          
        }
        })
     
     /*gsap-animation-end*/

jQuery(".cstm-filter-btn-main").click(function(){
    jQuery(".filter-button-cstm").toggleClass("main-button-filter");

    if (jQuery(this).hasClass("active-filter-button")) {

    }
    else
    {
    jQuery(".cstm-filter-btn-main p").text("SHOW FILTERS");
    }

});
jQuery(window).scroll(function (event) {
    var scroll = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
    jQuery('.cstm-filter-btn-main').toggleClass('remove-btn',
     //add 'ok' class when div position match or exceeds else remove the 'ok' class.
      scroll >= jQuery('.dn-paginator-container').offset().top
    );
});

 // google analytics code
  
//search 
    jQuery(".dn-search-field-container").on("keypress", function(event) {
  
    var searchValue = jQuery('input[name="query"]').val();
     if (event.which === 13) {
  dataLayer.push({
    event: "view_search_results",
    gtm: {uniqueEventId: 0, start: 1672656192033, priorityId: 2},
    eventModel: {search_term: searchValue}
     });
}
  
    });
  
jQuery(".dn-form .dn-form-field-inline .dn-btn-label").on("click", function() {
  // Send data to Google Analytics
  if (typeof dataLayer !== "undefined") {
    var leadId = Date.now();
    dataLayer.push({
      event: "subscribe",
      Lead_ID: leadId
    });
  } else {
    var leadId = Date.now();
    gtag('event', 'subscribe', {
      'Lead ID': leadId
    });
  }
});
 jQuery(".registration-form-data li.dn-form-action-footer .dn-btn").on("click", function() {
  // Send data to Google Analytics
  if (typeof dataLayer !== "undefined") {
    dataLayer.push({
      'event': 'Registration',
      'Lead ID': Date.now()
    });
  }
});
jQuery(".contact-form-sec-cstm li.dn-form-footer-actions .dn-btn .dn-btn-label").on("click", function() {
    var timestamp = new Date().getTime();
    dataLayer.push({
      event: 'Contact Form Submit',
      'Lead ID': 'Form_Submit_' + timestamp
    });
});

 //add_to_cart
jQuery("#add_to_cart_button").on("click", function() {
  var product_id = jQuery(this).closest('.dn-product').data("product-id");
  var product_name = jQuery('span#blank_product_title').text();
  var product_name_id = jQuery('span#blank_product_code').text();
  var product_title_and_code = product_name + ' - ' + product_name_id;
  var product_price = parseFloat(jQuery("div#price .dn-price-container").text().replace(/[^0-9\.]+/g, ""));
  var product_quantity = parseInt(jQuery("input#sizes_0_qty").val(), 10);
  var variant = jQuery("#sizes_0_optId option:selected").text();
  // Push the data to the data layer
  if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
    dataLayer.push({
      event: "add_to_cart",
      ecommerce: {
        currencyCode: "AUD",
         value: product_price,
        items: [
          {
            id: product_id,
            name: product_title_and_code,
            brand: jQuery(this).closest('.dn-product').data("product-brand"), 
            category: jQuery(this).closest('.dn-product').data("product-category"),
            variant: variant,
            price: product_price,
            quantity: product_quantity
          }
        ]
      },
      gtm: {
        uniqueEventId: Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000000000000000)
      }
    });
  }
});

jQuery(document).on("click", "#dn_cart_over_right_popup .dn-shopping-cart-container.dn-behaviour .dn-shopping-cart-actions .dn-btn-cart", function() {
  var productName = jQuery(".dn-line-item-details-name div").first().text().trim();
  var priceString = jQuery(".dn-line-item-price").first().text().trim();
  dataLayer.push({
    event: "view_cart",
    ecommerce: {
      currency: "AUD",
      value: price,
      items: [

          item_name: productName,
          price: price,
        }
      ]

//Remove from cart
jQuery(document).on("click", ".dn-checkout-c-product-remove", function() {
  var productContainer = jQuery(this).closest(".dn-checkout-row");
  var name = productContainer.find(".dn-checkout-c-product-name").text().trim();
  var priceText = productContainer.find(".dn-checkout-c-total.dn-checkout-c-lv.dn-checkout-c-price-field span").eq(0).text().trim();
  var price = parseFloat(priceText.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, ''));
  var qtyText = productContainer.find(".dn-checkout-c-qty.dn-checkout-c-lv span").text().trim();
  var qty = parseInt(qtyText.match(/\d+/)[0], 10);
  var color = productContainer.find(".dn-checkout-c-options .dn-checkout-c-o-field:nth-child(1) span").text().trim();
  var sizeWithQty = productContainer.find(".dn-checkout-c-options .dn-checkout-c-o-field:nth-child(2) span").text().trim();
  var size = sizeWithQty.split(' ')[0].trim();
  dataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null }); // Clear the previous ecommerce object.
  dataLayer.push({
    event: "remove_from_cart",
    ecommerce: {
      currency: "AUD",
      value: price,
      items: [
        {
          item_name: name,
          index: 0,
          item_category2: color,
          item_variant: size,
          price: price,
          quantity: qty 
        }
      ]
    }
  });
});
// Being Checkout
jQuery("#checkout_button").on("click", function() {
  var productName = jQuery('.dn-d-cart-line-item-details a:first-child').text().trim();
  var productBrand = jQuery(".dn-product-brand").text();
  var productCategory = jQuery(".dn-breadcrumb-link:last-child").text();
  var optionsDiv = jQuery('.dn-d-cart-line-item-options');
  var optionsText = optionsDiv.text().trim();
  var optionsArray = optionsText.split(',');
  var sizeInput = optionsArray[1].split(':')[1].trim();
  var size = sizeInput.replace(/\s/g, ''); 
  var productPrice = parseFloat(jQuery(".dn-price-container").text().replace(/[^0-9.]+/g, ""));
  var productQuantity = parseInt(jQuery(".dn-size-qty-container .dn-styled").val(), 10);
  var couponCode = ""; 
  dataLayer.push({
    event: "begin_checkout",
    ecommerce: {
      currencyCode: "AUD",
      value:productPrice,
      items: [
        {
          name: productName,
          variant: size,
          quantity: productQuantity,
          price: productPrice
        }
      ]
    }
  });
});

  var selectedText = jQuery("#sizes_0_optId option:selected").text();
  var productPrice = parseFloat(jQuery("#price .dn-price-container").text().replace(/[^0-9\.]+/g,""));
  var productQty= jQuery('#sizes_0_qty').val();
  var prdctqty = parseInt(productQty);
        
  var selectedCell = document.querySelector(".dn-color-panel-cell.dn-selected");
 var selectedColor = selectedCell.getAttribute("title");
 dataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });  // Clear the previous ecommerce object.
 
dataLayer.push({
    event: "start_designing",
    ecommerce: {
      currency: "AUD",
      value: productPrice,
      items: [
        {
          item_id: productId,
          item_name: productName,
          index: 0,
          item_brand: productBrand,
          item_category: productCategory,
          item_category2: selectedColor,
          item_list_id: productId,
          item_list_name: productName,
          item_variant: selectedText,
          price: productPrice,
          quantity: prdctqty
        }
      ]
    }
  });
});

var item_prc = parseFloat(formattedPrice);

//purchase   
jQuery(document).on('click', '.confirm-data-cstm .dn-widget .dn-checkout-page form.dn-behaviour.dn-with-disable-overlay .dn-form-footer-actions .dn-btn', function() {
  var shipping = parseFloat(jQuery(".dn-checkout-cart.dn-checkout-with-table .dn-subtotal-price").text().trim().replace(/[^0-9\.]+/g, ""));
  var taxString = jQuery(".dn-shipping-tax-price").text().trim();
  var tax = parseFloat(taxString.replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g,""));
  var productNames = [];
  var productVariants = [];
  jQuery(".dn-line-item-details-name").each(function() {
    productNames.push(jQuery(this).text().trim());
  });
  jQuery(".dn-line-item-details-options").each(function() {
    productVariants.push(jQuery(this).text().trim());
  });
  var productName = productNames.join(", ");
  var productVariant = productVariants.join(", ");
  var productBrand = jQuery(".dn-product-brand").text().trim();
  var productCategory = jQuery(".dn-breadcrumb-link:last-child").text().trim();
  var productPrice = parseFloat(jQuery(".dn-total-price").text().replace(/[^0-9\.]+/g, ""));
  var productQuantity = parseInt(jQuery(".dn-line-item-thumbnail span").text());
  var size = jQuery(".dn-line-item-details-options").text().trim();
  var color = jQuery(".dn-line-item-thumbnail .dn-swatch .dn-swatch-label").text().trim();
  dataLayer.push({
    'event': 'purchase',
    'ecommerce': {
          'revenue': productPrice,
          'tax': tax,
          'shipping': shipping,
          'currencyCode': 'AUD',
          'items': [{
          'name': productName,
          'variant': size,
          'price': productPrice,
          'quantity': productQuantity
        }]
    }
  });
});

//trigger the scroll
jQuery(window).scroll();
(function() {
  
  var parent = document.querySelector(".range-slider");
  if(!parent) return;
  var
    rangeS = parent.querySelectorAll("input[type=range]"),
    numberS = parent.querySelectorAll("input[type=number]");
  rangeS.forEach(function(el) {
    el.oninput = function() {
      var slide1 = parseFloat(rangeS[0].value),
            slide2 = parseFloat(rangeS[1].value);
      if (slide1 > slide2) {
                [slide1, slide2] = [slide2, slide1];
        // var tmp = slide2;
        // slide2 = slide1;
        // slide1 = tmp;
      }
      numberS[0].value = slide1;
      numberS[1].value = slide2;
    }
  });
  numberS.forEach(function(el) {
    el.oninput = function() {
            var number1 = parseFloat(numberS[0].value),
                    number2 = parseFloat(numberS[1].value);
            
      if (number1 > number2) {
        var tmp = number1;
        numberS[0].value = number2;
        numberS[1].value = tmp;
      }
      rangeS[0].value = number1;
      rangeS[1].value = number2;
    }
  });
  })();
  
  
});
  
  
/*topscroll-end*/      
</script>

  function appendCustomStyleSheets(nodeEl) {
    var sheets = document.styleSheets;
    for(var i=0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
      var sheet = sheets[i];
      if(sheet.href != null && sheet.href.trim() != "" && !sheet.href.includes("bundlev3")) {
        nodeEl.append('<link rel="stylesheet" href="' + sheet.href + '" type="text/css" media="all">\n');
      }
    }
  }
  function initPage() {
    if(typeof dnBehaviours !== 'undefined') {
      dnBehaviours.bind(null, false);
    } else {
      $dnj(document.body).addClass("dn-behaviours-bound");
    }
    $dnj.ajaxSetup({
      headers: { 'X-CSRF-Token': dnCSRFToken }
    });

    var replacement = document.createElement("div");
    replacement.innerHTML = addStylesNode.textContent;
    document.body.appendChild(replacement)
    addStylesNode.parentElement.removeChild(addStylesNode);

    dnInitLazyLoad();
  }
